Michael Keaton is a renowned actor known for his exceptional acting skills and captivating performances in a wide array of movies. In this movie roundup article, we delve into the remarkable career of this talented actor, highlighting some of his most memorable films. From his breakout role in Tim Burton's "Beetlejuice" to his Oscar-nominated performance in "Birdman, " read on to explore the diverse filmography of Hollywood star, Michael Keaton. Whether you're a fan of his classic comedies or captivated by his recent dramatic performances, this roundup is sure to keep you entertained and enthralled.

## 1. [A Different Approach (1978)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/a-different-approach-1978?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=a-different-approach-1978&utm_term=a-different-approach-1978)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/a-different-approach-1978?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=a-different-approach-1978&amp;utm_term=a-different-approach-1978"><img alt="a-different-approach-tt0077434-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/a-different-approach-tt0077434-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"A Different Approach" (1978) is a groundbreaking short film that addresses the often overlooked issue of employment discrimination against people with disabilities. This compelling educational film features a captivating performance by Michael Keaton, who leads an all-star cast in making a strong case for hiring the handicapped in the workplace. The ingenious plot unfolds as a board observes the movie, which takes an unconventional approach by incorporating suggestions from Hollywood personalities. With its wit and charm, the film sheds light on the benefits of including people with disabilities in the workforce, offering a refreshing perspective on the topic. "A Different Approach" is noteworthy not only for its subject matter but also for its accomplished director, Fern Field, and star-studded cast, including Beverly Archer, Carl Ballantine, and Sorrell Booke. With its engaging storytelling and powerful message, this hidden gem has been nominated for an Oscar and remains a timeless classic in the realm of short films. 



<br>

- Genres: Short
- Runtime: 21min
- Directed by: Fern Field
- Starring: Beverly Archer, Carl Ballantine, Sorrell Booke
- Box Office:
- IMDb Rating: 7.5
- Awards: Nominated for 1 Oscar, 1 nomination total
- Similar: Studs Lonigan, Clean and Sober, Report to Murphy, The Squeeze, Rabbit Test, Night Shift, Gung Ho, Mary Hartman, Mary Hartman, Fernwood Tonight, The Merry Gentleman, Serial, Working Stiffs

## 2. [Rabbit Test (1978)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/rabbit-test-1978?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=rabbit-test-1978&utm_term=rabbit-test-1978)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/rabbit-test-1978?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=rabbit-test-1978&amp;utm_term=rabbit-test-1978"><img alt="rabbit-test-tt0078133-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/rabbit-test-tt0078133-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Rabbit Test" is a 1978 comedy directed by Joan Rivers that takes an unconventional approach to storytelling. The film follows the peculiar life of Lionel, who finds himself in an extraordinary situation after a one-night stand on top of a pinball table - he becomes the world's first pregnant man! This bizarre turn of events creates a rollercoaster ride of humor and unexpected challenges for the central character, with comedic elements at the forefront of the narrative. The movie is a product of a collaboration between Rivers and Jay Redack, featuring a talented cast of actors including Billy Crystal, Alex Rocco, and Joan Prather. With a runtime of 1h 24min and a PG content rating, "Rabbit Test" offers viewers a unique blend of humor and curiosity, while at the same time, it subtly delves into themes of race and cultural understanding with elements like blackface, minstrel show, and racist humor. Through its wacky plotline, the film has been recognized with a nomination for an award and has been compared to similar comedies of that era. Though not boasting huge box office success, the movie stands out for its distinct narrative and unforgettable title, providing viewers with a memorable viewing experience. For those looking for a offbeat comedy with a twist, "Rabbit Test" is a film that pushes the boundaries of conventional storytelling and promises an entertaining escape. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy
- Rated: PG
- Runtime: 1h 24min
- Directed by: Joan Rivers
- Starring: Billy Crystal, Alex Rocco, Joan Prather
- Box Office:
- IMDb Rating: 3.1
- Awards: Awards, 1 nomination
- Similar: Breaking Up Is Hard to Do, Keep on Truckin', SST: Death Flight, Human Feelings, Report to Murphy, Studs Lonigan, All's Fair, The Squeeze, Touch and Go, Mr. Saturday Night, Working Stiffs, Memories of Me

## 3. [Night Shift (1982)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/night-shift-1982?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=night-shift-1982&utm_term=night-shift-1982)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/night-shift-1982?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=night-shift-1982&amp;utm_term=night-shift-1982"><img alt="night-shift-tt0084412-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/night-shift-tt0084412-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Night Shift" is a 1982 comedy directed by Ron Howard, starring Henry Winkler, Michael Keaton, and Shelley Long. The film follows a mild-mannered morgue attendant as he takes up the night shift. Along with his eccentric coworker, they convince him to lead a prostitution ring out of the morgue. The movie features a talented ensemble cast in a lighthearted story that explores unusual friendships and unique business endeavors amidst the eccentric backdrop of a morgue. "Night Shift" boasts a rich blend of humor, charm, and unpredictability, making it a cult classic in the world of comedy cinema. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 1h 46min
- Directed by: Ron Howard

## 4. [Mr. Mom (1983)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/mr-mom-1983?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=mr-mom-1983&utm_term=mr-mom-1983)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/mr-mom-1983?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=mr-mom-1983&amp;utm_term=mr-mom-1983"><img alt="mr-mom-tt0085970-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/mr-mom-tt0085970-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Mr. Mom" is a heartwarming comedy-drama from 1983 that tells the story of a husband who loses his job and finds himself taking on the responsibilities of a stay-at-home dad. The unexpected role reversal challenges him to navigate the daily life of caring for three young children while his wife returns to the workforce. This charming tale, directed by Stan Dragoti and written by John Hughes, explores the often humorous and frustrating world of a stay-at-home husband grappling with a new kind of yuppie lifestyle. Michael Keaton stars as the befuddled husband trying to manage the unexpected challenges of parenthood, while Teri Garr plays the supportive but equally overwhelmed wife. The film also serves as a comedic showcase for the talents of young actors Frederick Koehler and Martin Starr. "Mr. Mom" has been well-received by both audiences and critics alike, garnering awards and recognition for its engaging story and memorable performances. The movie is a delightful blend of comedy and drama, with moments of pure laughter and heart-tugging sincerity. As a study of role reversal and the importance of family, "Mr. Mom" stands the test of time as an enjoyable and thought-provoking film. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy, Drama
- Rated: PG
- Runtime: 1h 31min
- Directed by: Stan Dragoti
- Starring: Michael Keaton, Teri Garr, Frederick Koehler
- Box Office:
 - Gross USA: $64,783,827
 - Opening Weekend USA: $947,197
 - Cumulative Worldwide Gross: $64,783,827
- IMDb Rating: 6.6
- Awards: Awards, 1 win & 1 nomination

## 6. [Johnny Dangerously (1984)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/johnny-dangerously-1984?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=johnny-dangerously-1984&utm_term=johnny-dangerously-1984)

Join Michael Keaton as Johnny Dangerously, a small-time newspaper boy in the 1930s who finds himself caught in the world of organized crime. When medical bills for his neurotic mother spiral out of control, Johnny is forced to take drastic measures in order to provide for her. Plunged into the dark world of gangsters and nightclubs, Keaton's charismatic presence sets the tone for a whirlwind of laughter and suspense amidst the backdrop of crime and corruption. With its talented ensemble cast, including Joe Piscopo and Marilu Henner, and the creative direction by Amy Heckerling, "Johnny Dangerously" delivers a captivating blend of comedy and crime that is sure to have you glued to your seat. Don't miss this must-see classic that earned an IMDb rating of 6.5.

"Comic Relief" is a captivating 1986 comedy special, hosted by the legendary trio, Robin Williams, Billy Crystal, and Whoopi Goldberg. The first in a series of shows, this film utilizes the power of humor to raise awareness for poverty. Featuring a host of comedians, including George Carlin, Billy Crystal, and Whoopi Goldberg, the live audience was treated to an assortment of stand-up sets and sketches. With a runtime of 2 hours and 8 minutes, "Comic Relief" offers a memorable and entertaining event that successfully blends comedy with a charitable cause, leaving a lasting impact on viewers. Filled with unforgettable performances, the movie boasts an impressive 7.4 IMDb rating and features an all-star line-up of stars and directors. "Comic Relief" is a must-watch for any comedy enthusiast and a perfect blend of humor and heart.

## 9. [Touch and Go (1986)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/touch-and-go-1986?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=touch-and-go-1986&utm_term=touch-and-go-1986)

"Touch and Go" (1986) is a compelling and witty mix of comedy, drama, and romance that will keep you on the edge of your seat. Starring Michael Keaton and Maria Conchita Alonso, and directed by Robert Mandel, the film follows the life of an ice hockey star who encounters a troubled youth gang, leading to an unexpected romance with the gang member's mother. As the story unfolds, a dramatic confrontation with the gang leaders ensues, providing a gripping narrative that will keep you hooked for the full runtime of 1h 41min. This entertaining film boasts an impressive ensemble cast and is perfect for those who want an engaging cinematic experience filled with witty banter, unexpected romance, and action-packed confrontations. With its captivating plot and talented cast, "Touch and Go" stands as a notable entry in the comedy-drama genre. Its captivating storyline makes it a worthwhile movie choice for audiences of all ages and preferences. The film's connection to other critically acclaimed movies such as "Night Shift", "One Good Cop", and "Johnny Dangerously" highlights its strong presence in the world of cinema and its deserving recognition. Don't miss this entertaining movie, as it delivers an unforgettable fusion of laughter, heartbreak, and drama that will leave you wanting more.

## 10. [Gung Ho (1986)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/gung-ho-1986?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=gung-ho-1986&utm_term=gung-ho-1986)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/gung-ho-1986?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=gung-ho-1986&amp;utm_term=gung-ho-1986"><img alt="gung-ho-tt0091159-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/gung-ho-tt0091159-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Gung Ho" (1986) is a spirited comedy-drama directed by Ron Howard, starring Michael Keaton, Gedde Watanabe, and George Wendt. The film delves into the complex dynamics of cultural clashes and the automobile industry as American workers adapt to the Japanese management at a newly acquired car factory. Set in the 1980s, this feel-good movie expertly combines witty humor with thoughtful insight into work relationships and the American dream. Audiences will appreciate the engaging performances and relatable storyline that showcases the power of determination and camaraderie in overcoming obstacles. Experience the laughter and heart as "Gung Ho" takes you on a memorable journey of teamwork and transformation.

The film's exploration of home invasion and the lengths to which individuals may go to achieve their goals serves as a potent cautionary tale. Furthermore, the movie's portrayal of the complex dynamics between landlords and tenants delves into the underlying tensions and power struggles that often accompany property disputes. With its blend of suspense, psychological drama, and captivating performances, "Pacific Heights" stands as a prime example of the thriller genre. Meanwhile, LaPaglia's character is a volatile and dangerous adversary, making for an electrifying game of cat and mouse between the protagonist and antagonist. By combining the raw energy of action sequences with the poignant character development of family drama, Gould creates a compelling and authentic cinematic experience that will resonate with viewers long after the final scene. As Bob's health deteriorates, he struggles to come to terms with his own mortality while trying to leave a lasting legacy for his child. The film explores themes of love, loss, and the importance of living life to the fullest. With a runtime of 1 hour and 57 minutes, "My Life" is an emotional rollercoaster that encourages viewers to reflect on the value of life and the preciousness of our relationships. ## 117. [The Flash (2023)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-flash-2023?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=the-flash-2023&utm_term=the-flash-2023)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-flash-2023?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=the-flash-2023&amp;utm_term=the-flash-2023"><img alt="the-flash-tt0439572-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/the-flash-tt0439572-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"The Flash" (2023) is a high-octane action-adventure film based on the iconic DC Comics character. The story follows Barry Allen, played by Ezra Miller, a young man who gains superhuman speed after being struck by lightning. As he races through time to save his loved ones, Allen unknowingly alters the timeline, creating a world without superheroes and must race against time to restore the original timeline and save the future. Directed by Andy Muschietti, this thrilling film also stars Michael Keaton as Batman and Sasha Calle as Supergirl, with an original screenplay by Christina Hodson, John Francis Daley, and Jonathan Goldstein. Filled with fantastical elements and breathtaking visual effects, "The Flash" promises an exhilarating ride through the DC Extended Universe. The movie is a part of the DCEU and explores the multiverse concept, delving deeper into the world of DC Comics. Fans of the comic book franchise will be delighted by the movie's faithful adaptation and the reprise of beloved characters. Through its engaging storyline, stunning visuals, and outstanding performances, "The Flash" delivers an unforgettable cinematic experience. Don't miss this exciting entry into the DCEU, hitting theaters on June 16, 2023.
